38:2046:117003:15:15:86:334:665:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:counterfactuals in matching maximum score inequalities.
38:2047:117058:15:15:101:525:650:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:Table 3 reports the estimates with weights.  There are three specifications, each with different
38:2048:117154:15:15:86:525:635:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:weights. Note that the parameters multiply different explanatory variables across the three specifi-
38:2049:117254:15:15:86:525:620:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:cations, so the parameters have slightly different interpretations. However, the means and standard
38:2050:117353:15:14:86:525:605:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:deviations of the weighted HHI measures are qualitatively similar to those reported in Table 1 for the
38:2051:117455:14:15:86:180:591:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:baseline specification.
38:2052:117478:15:29:101:401:576:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:The first weighting scheme in Table 3 does not use sales data; it sets
38:2053:117548:29:0:222:244:547:10:g_d0_f10:10:g_d0_f8:wc=
38:2054:117551:0:14:314:319:554:10:g_d0_f8:10:g_d0_f8:1
38:2055:117552:14:0:248:385:540:10:g_d0_f8:10:g_d0_f10:# car parts for model in marketd
38:2056:117584:0:29:386:389:547:10:g_d0_f10:10:g_d0_f10:.
38:2057:117585:29:15:86:525:518:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:This scheme weights a car part on a car model with more parts in a component category less, in order
38:2058:117685:15:15:86:525:503:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:to equalized the contribution of car models to HHI calculations. The second weighting scheme uses
38:2059:117782:15:15:86:135:488:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:the weights
38:2060:117793:15:22:255:356:473:10:g_d0_f10:10:g_d0_f10:wc= sales of car model.
38:2061:117816:22:29:86:352:451:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:The third weighting scheme combines the previous two, as in
38:2062:117875:29:7:222:353:422:10:g_d0_f10:10:g_d0_f8:wc=sales of car model
38:2063:117896:7:0:248:385:415:10:g_d0_f8:10:g_d0_f10:# car parts for model in marketd
38:2064:117928:0:29:386:389:422:10:g_d0_f10:10:g_d0_f10:.
38:2065:117929:29:15:101:525:393:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:Compared to Table 1, Table 3 shows less of a role for supplier model specialization and much more
38:2066:118026:15:15:86:525:378:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:of a role for assembler model HHI specialization. In all three of the specifications, the lower bound for
38:2067:118131:15:15:86:525:363:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:the confidence region for supplier HHI model specification is negative and large in magnitude relative
38:2068:118233:15:15:86:525:348:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:to the+1normalization for supplier parent group specialization. The point estimate is negative in
38:2069:118330:15:15:86:525:333:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:two of the three specifications. In all three specifications, the upper bound of the confidence region for
38:2070:118436:15:15:86:525:318:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:assembler model specialization is unbounded. The point estimate for assembler model specialization
38:2071:118534:15:15:86:478:303:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:is unbounded in two specifications and still quite large, at 202, for the other specification.
38:2072:118628:15:15:101:525:288:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:Also compared to Table 1, there is now statistical uncertainty about the sign of supplier brand
38:2073:118723:15:15:86:525:273:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:specialization, although the point estimate is about the same as for parent group specialization, which
38:2074:118826:15:15:86:525:258:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:is normalized to+1. Similarly to Table 1, 0 is still in the confidence regions for assembler parent
38:2075:118925:15:15:86:224:243:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:group and brand specialization.
38:2076:118956:15:37:101:454:228:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:Overall, I emphasize Table 1 in the main text because of its higher statistical fit.
38:2077:119040:37:25:86:507:191:14:g_d0_f3:14:g_d0_f3:D  Benefits to Domestic Suppliers From Foreign Assemblers
38:2078:119097:25:15:86:525:166:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:European and North American countries have imposed formal and political-pressure based trade
38:2079:119189:15:15:86:525:151:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:barriers to imports of automobiles from Asia.  Consequently, most Asian assemblers who sell cars
38:2080:119285:15:15:86:525:136:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:in Europe and North America also assemble cars in Europe and North America.  While some car
38:2081:119376:15:15:86:525:121:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:parts are imported from Asia, Asian assembly plants in Europe and North America use many parts
38:2082:119470:15:15:86:525:106:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:produced locally as well (perhaps because of more political pressure).  As Klier and Rubenstein
38:2083:119565:15:0:86:525:91:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:(2008) document for Asian assemblers in North America, a key part of operating an assembly plant
39:2084:119663:0:15:86:300:695:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:is developing a network of high-quality suppliers.
39:2085:119713:15:15:101:525:680:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:Despite some occasional quality setbacks, the magazineConsumer Reportsand other sources
39:2086:119800:15:15:86:525:665:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:routinely record that brands with headquarters in Asia (Japan, Korea) have higher quality automobiles
39:2087:119901:15:15:86:525:650:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:than brands with headquarters in Europe or North America. The parts supplied to higher-quality cars
39:2088:120000:15:15:86:525:635:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:must typically also be of higher quality. Liker and Wu (2000) document that suppliers to Japanese-
39:2089:120098:15:15:86:525:620:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:owned brands in the US produce fewer parts requiring reworking or scrapping, for example. Because
39:2090:120195:15:14:86:525:605:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:of this emphasis on quality, the suppliers to, say, Toyota undergo a rigorous screening and training
39:2091:120295:14:15:86:525:591:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:program, the Supplier Development Program, before producing a large volume of car parts for Toyota
39:2092:120393:15:15:86:525:576:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:(Langfield-Smith and Greenwood, 1998). Indeed, there is a hierarchy of suppliers, with more trusted
39:2093:120492:15:15:86:525:561:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:Toyota suppliers being allowed to supply more car parts (Kamath and Liker, 1994; Liker and Wu,
39:2094:120586:15:15:86:113:546:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:2000).
39:2095:120592:15:15:101:525:531:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:It is possible that the need by Asian assemblers for higher-quality suppliers benefits the entire
39:2096:120689:15:15:86:525:516:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:domestic supplier bases in Europe and North America. If a supplier is of high-enough quality to deal
39:2097:120789:15:15:86:525:501:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:with an Asian assembler, non-Asian assemblers that also source parts from that supplier may also
39:2098:120885:15:15:86:525:486:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:benefit. If this potential effect is causal (the suppliers were not of sufficiently high quality before the
39:2099:120992:15:15:86:525:471:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:Asian assemblers’ entry), it is evidence that trade barriers that promote Asian-owned assembly plants
39:2100:121093:15:15:86:525:456:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:in Europe and North America may indirectly aid non-Asian (domestic) assemblers, as those producers
39:2101:121191:15:15:86:525:441:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:now have access to higher-quality suppliers. This is an underexplored channel by which foreign-direct
39:2102:121292:15:15:86:525:426:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:investment in assembly plants may raise the quality of producers in upstream markets. Indeed, there
39:2103:121391:15:15:86:525:411:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:is evidence in the management literature that Asian assemblers do causally upgrade the quality of
39:2104:121488:15:15:86:525:396:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:their suppliers: the Supplier Development Program mentioned above, for example (Langfield-Smith
39:2105:121583:15:15:86:187:381:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:and Greenwood, 1998).
39:2106:121604:15:15:101:525:366:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:This section complements the management literature by providing evidence from sorting in the
39:2107:121696:15:15:86:525:351:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:market for car parts that might be consistent with suppliers to Asian assemblers being higher quality
39:2108:121797:15:14:86:525:336:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:than other suppliers. Measures of car part quality by individual suppliers are presumably observed
39:2109:121895:14:15:86:525:322:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:by assemblers, but are not publicly available. In this section, a measure of quality will be a supplier’s
39:2110:122000:15:15:86:525:307:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:share of the market for supplying parts to Asian assemblers. If Asian assemblers together demand
39:2111:122096:15:15:86:525:292:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:100 parts in a particular component category, and one supplier sells 30 of them, its quality measure
39:2112:122196:15:29:86:445:277:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:will be 0.30. In notation, one aspect of an observable firm typejsfor a supplier is
39:2113:122279:29:7:198:390:248:10:g_d0_f10:10:g_d0_f8:jsAsia=# Asian assembler parts supplied
39:2114:122318:7:0:232:408:241:10:g_d0_f8:10:g_d0_f8:total # Asian assembler parts all suppliers
39:2115:122361:0:29:410:413:248:10:g_d0_f10:10:g_d0_f10:.
39:2116:122362:29:15:86:525:219:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:This is not a specialization measure, as a firm could sell many parts to Asian assemblers and many
39:2117:122460:15:15:86:525:204:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:parts to non-Asian assemblers. This quality measurejsAsiais treated as an aspect of observable firm
39:2118:122559:15:15:86:525:189:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:typejsof a supplier. If it were recomputed for new portfoliosΦwithout interactions in a valuation
39:2119:122656:15:15:86:525:174:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:function, it would difference out of the matching maximum score inequalities (10). Instead, the vector
39:2120:122758:15:15:86:525:159:10:g_d0_f10:10:g_d0_f4:X(js,Ψ)contains a new element that is the interaction of the above Asian quality measure with
39:2121:122851:15:28:86:415:144:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:specialization by the continent headquarters of the brand, discussed earlier:
39:2122:122928:28:27:219:392:116:10:g_d0_f10:10:g_d0_f10:XAsiaCont(js,Ψ) =jsAsia·XCont(js,Ψ).
39:2123:122964:27:0:86:525:89:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:The interpretation of the corresponding supplier parameter inθ, if it is estimated to be negative, is
40:2124:123067:0:15:86:525:695:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:that suppliers with higherjsAsia(greater shares of the industry for supplying Asian assemblers) gain
40:2125:123167:15:15:86:525:680:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:less benefit from selling car parts to only one continent of assembler than suppliers with lowerjsAsia.
40:2126:123270:15:15:86:525:665:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:Thus, suppliers with higher Asian shares can go out and win business from non-Asian assemblers,
40:2127:123365:15:15:86:525:650:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:which is consistent with those firms have a competitive edge (possibly from higher quality parts) over
40:2128:123467:15:15:86:525:635:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:other suppliers. The empirical pattern in the data might be that suppliers with highjsAsiahave diverse
40:2129:123569:15:15:86:525:620:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:(across continents of assembler origin) portfolios of car parts that they supply. This diversity might
40:2130:123671:15:14:86:235:605:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:be interpreted as a sign of quality.
40:2131:123707:14:15:101:525:591:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:Even if the parameter onXAsiaCont(js,Ψ)is negative and economically large in magnitude, it does
40:2132:123802:15:15:86:525:576:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:not prove that the presence of Asian assemblers causally upgrades the quality of suppliers in Europe
40:2133:123902:15:15:86:525:561:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:and North America. It could have been that the suppliers with highjsAsiawere of high quality before
40:2134:124001:15:15:86:525:546:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:the creation of plants outside Asia by Asian assemblers. However, when combined with the evidence
40:2135:124098:15:15:86:525:531:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:from the management literature about supplier development programs, it does seem as if some portion
40:2136:124197:15:15:86:427:516:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:of supplier quality differences are due to the presence of the Asian assemblers.
40:2137:124277:15:15:101:525:501:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:A separate concern is that this approach treatsjsAsiaas an economically exogenous characteristic,
40:2138:124374:15:15:86:525:486:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:rather than recomputing the Asian market share for counterfactual sets of tradesΦin the right
40:2139:124467:15:15:86:525:471:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:sides of matching maximum score inequalities. I have explored the specification where notationally
40:2140:124565:15:15:86:525:456:10:g_d0_f10:10:g_d0_f4:jsAsiais replaced byXAsia(js,Ψ), which is recomputed for counterfactual sets of tradesΨ.  The
40:2141:124658:15:15:86:526:441:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:corresponding point estimate on the interaction is≈0, with a wide confidence interval in terms
40:2142:124752:15:15:86:525:426:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:of economic magnitudes.  An explanation for the point estimate close to 0 is that a new effect is
40:2143:124849:15:15:86:525:411:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:introduced to the model: the inequalities ask why more suppliers do not choose to supply parts to
40:2144:124946:15:15:86:525:396:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:Asian assemblers if there is some quality upgrade from doing so?  A reason outside of the model
40:2145:125041:15:15:86:525:381:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:why this does not happen is the fixed cost of having an additional supplier participate in a supplier
40:2146:125142:15:15:86:525:366:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:development program. Having explored an alternative, I return to the preferred specification, where
40:2147:125241:15:15:86:492:351:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:a supplier’s competitive advantage is an economically exogenous supplier characteristicjsAsia.
40:2148:125335:15:14:101:525:336:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:Table 4 presents the point estimates from the preferred specification. The other covariates are the
40:2149:125434:14:15:86:525:322:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:assembler and supplier specialization measures in Table 1, which have similar point estimates. The
40:2150:125532:15:15:86:525:307:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f8:scale normalization is still on parent group specialization. With the interaction termXAsiaCont(js,Ψ)
40:2151:125633:15:15:86:525:292:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:involving continent specialization, the normalization can only be understood by substituting a typ-
40:2152:125732:15:15:86:525:277:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:ical value forjsAsiainto the interaction termXAsiaCont(js,Ψ)and comparing also the coefficient on
40:2153:125829:15:15:86:292:262:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:continent specialization without an interaction.
40:2154:125877:15:15:101:525:247:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:The new addition to Table 4 is the estimate on the interaction termXAsia(js,Ψ), which would use
40:2155:125972:15:15:86:525:232:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:an estimated decrease in the importance of specialization at the continent-of-brand level for suppliers
40:2156:126075:15:15:86:525:217:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:to Asian brands’ assembly plants in Europe and North America as evidence that suppliers to Asian
40:2157:126171:15:15:86:525:202:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:assemblers have higher quality. These suppliers possibly can win business from non-Asian assemblers.
40:2158:126271:15:15:86:525:187:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:The estimate of the parameter onXAsia(js,Ψ)is -0.261 and the mean and standard deviation ofjsAsia,
40:2159:126369:15:15:86:525:172:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:not listed in the table, are 0.069 and 0.102, respectively. Therefore, a one-standard deviation change
40:2160:126471:15:15:86:525:157:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:injsAsiacreates a change of−0.261·0.102 =−0.0266in the coefficient on the degree of specialization
40:2161:126569:15:15:86:525:142:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:at the continent-of-brand level. A car parts supplier with a market share among Asian assemblers
40:2162:126665:15:15:86:525:127:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:that is one standard deviation higher than the mean, a share of 0.171, will have a total coefficient on
40:2163:126768:15:15:86:526:112:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:continent-of-brand specialization of+1.03−0.261·0.171 = 0.985, or approximately 1. This is a small
40:2164:126866:15:0:86:525:97:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:magnitude change. Now that the confidence region for the interaction parameter is huge, from -30 to
41:2165:126967:0:15:86:266:695:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:32. The data do not pin down this effect.
41:2166:127008:15:15:101:525:680:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:With a bigger in absolute value and more precisely estimated effect, the interpretation would
41:2167:127101:15:15:86:525:665:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:have been that suppliers to Asian assemblers can go out and win business from non-Asian assemblers
41:2168:127199:15:15:86:525:650:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:as well, but suppliers to European and North American assemblers cannot win as much business
41:2169:127291:15:15:86:525:635:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:from assemblers from other continents. Thus, the evidence from sorting in the market for car parts
41:2170:127389:15:15:86:525:620:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:would have suggested that domestic suppliers to assemblers with headquarters in Asia are in a unique
41:2171:127489:15:14:86:525:605:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:competitive position, consistent with them having a quality advantage.  While the cross-sectional
41:2172:127586:14:15:86:525:591:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:empirical work alone cannot identify whether a quality increase causally occurred after the entry
41:2173:127683:15:15:86:525:576:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:of Asian-based assemblers to Europe and North America, the estimates and the evidence from the
41:2174:127777:15:15:86:525:561:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:management literature together would have suggested that having higher quality assemblers in Europe
41:2175:127876:15:15:86:525:546:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:and North America raises the quality of suppliers. Thus, in the automotive industry there might have
41:2176:127976:15:15:86:525:531:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:been evidence of indirect benefits to domestic suppliers and assemblers from the trade barriers that
41:2177:128076:15:38:86:385:516:10:g_d0_f4:10:g_d0_f4:encourage Asian assemblers to locate in Europe and North America.
